# Wrapper caller-burden ledger.
# Format: <theorem> <binder_index> <name> <category> <type-snippet>
#
# Mirrors `trust/baseline-caller-burden.txt` for the wrapper layer —
# every parameter the caller of an `equiv_<OP>_from_trust` (the
# wrappers under `ZiskFv/Equivalence/Compliance/*Exemplar.lean` +
# `DivPilot.lean`) is on the hook for. Adding, renaming, or
# reshaping any wrapper binder produces a diff that has to land
# alongside the refactor.
#
# Categories: validator | state | entry | range | match | bridge |
#             bus_shape | transpile | byte_chain | loose | row |
#             instance | other
#

# Category bridge: 22
# Category bus_shape: 509

# Category loose: 156
# Category match: 120
# Category other: 493
# Category range: 38
# Category row: 57

# Category transpile: 155
